15/**
16 * @fileoverview List formatting symbols for all locales.
17 *
18 * This file is autogenerated by script. See
19 * http://go/generate_list_symbols.py using --for_closure
20 * File generated from CLDR ver. 28
21 *
22 * To reduce the file size (which may cause issues in some JS
23 * developing environments), this file will only contain locales
24 * that are usually supported by Google products. It is a super
25 * set of 40 languages. The rest of the data can be found in another file
26 * named "listsymbolsext.js", which will be generated at the same
27 * time as this file.
28 * Before checkin, this file could have been manually edited. This is
29 * to incorporate changes before we could correct CLDR. All manual
30 * modification must be documented in this section, and should be
31 * removed after those changes land to CLDR.
32 */
